Paviot,A. Pisani,D. Potter,G. W. Pratt,S. Quai,M. Radovich,K. Rojas,W. Roster,S. Sacquegna,M. Sahlén,D. B. Sanders,E. Sarpa,A. Schneider,D. Sciotti,E. Sellentin,L. C. Smith,J. G. Sorce,K. Tanidis,C. Tao,F. Tarsitano,G. Testera,R. Teyssier,S. Tosi,A. Troja,D. Vergani,F. Vernizzi,G. Verza,P. Vielzeuf,S. Vinciguerra,N. A. Walton,A. H. Wright*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文评估了Euclid任务中利用高阶相关函数（特别是星系功率谱和三谱）提取宇宙学信息的潜力，通过基于Flagship I模拟的合成Hα星系样本验证了微扰理论预测，并表明加入三谱信息可显著提升关键宇宙学参数约束精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶相关函数（如三谱）能提供超出标准2点统计（如功率谱）的宇宙学信息；Euclid巡天将产生大量高质量光谱数据，亟需评估其高阶统计潜力。

Method: 使用基于Flagship I模拟的Hα星系合成星表，在实空间与红移空间中全面验证了一圈级功率谱与树级三谱的微扰理论预测；采用与先前功率谱研究一致的k-cut，并结合非线性偏置模型分析。

Result: 在合理k_max截断下，三谱可提供无偏宇宙学约束；加入三谱后，对σ8和Ωm的约束提升达30%，整体FOM提升约2.5倍；同时首次详细刻画了Hα发射体的非线性偏置行为。

Conclusion: 三谱是充分挖掘Euclid数据宇宙学价值的关键工具；当前微扰理论建模在适当尺度范围内可靠；Hα星系偏置需更精细建模，尤其在低红移。

Abstract: Higher-order correlation functions of the large-scale galaxy distribution offer access to information beyond that contained in standard 2-point statistics such as the power spectrum. In this work we assess this potential for the $\textit{Euclid}$ mission using synthetic catalogues of H$α$ galaxies based on the 54 $\, h^{-3} \, {\rm Gpc}^3$ Flagship I simulation, designed to reproduce the $\textit{Euclid}$ spectroscopic sample. We comprehensively validate the one-loop galaxy power spectrum and tree-level bispectrum predictions from perturbation theory in both real and redshift space. Assuming scale cuts consistent with our previous power spectrum study on the same catalogues, this modelling yields unbiased cosmological constraints for the bispectrum up to $k_{\rm max} = 0.15\,\, h \, {\rm Mpc}^{-1}$ in real space and $0.08 \, (0.1)\,\, h \, {\rm Mpc}^{-1}$ at the lowest (highest) redshift, corresponding to $z=0.9$ ($z=1.8$), for the monopole and quadrupole in redshift space using statistical uncertainties corresponding to the full simulation volume. With these scale cuts, adding bispectrum information to the power spectrum improves constraints on the amplitude of scalar perturbations and the matter density by up to 30 %, increasing the overall figure of merit for key cosmological parameters by a factor of about 2.5. Similar conclusions hold when statistical uncertainties are rescaled to a $\textit{Euclid}$-like volume, highlighting the importance of the bispectrum for fully exploiting the forthcoming $\textit{Euclid}$ data. Our analysis also provides the first detailed characterisation of the nonlinear bias model of H$α$ emitters, showing that bias relations calibrated on low-resolution \textit{N}-body simulations do not adequately describe the clustering of H$α$ galaxies at low redshift, whereas excursion-set and co-evolution relations for tidal biases remain accurate.

</details>


### [134] [Bayesian Model Comparison of $R_h=ct$ versus $Λ$CDM using HII galaxy Hubble diagram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28019)
*Yuva Himanshu Pallam,Shantanu Desai*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过贝叶斯模型比较，使用HII星系数据检验R_h=ct宇宙学模型与ΛCDM/wCDM模型的相对支持度；结果表明，在均匀先验下三者等效，在基于Planck的正态先验下R_h=ct显著优于ΛCDM、略优于wCDM。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验R_h=ct宇宙学模型相对于标准ΛCDM和wCDM模型的统计优劣，补充此前基于HII星系的分析。

Method: 采用贝叶斯模型比较方法，计算R_h=ct模型相对于平直ΛCDM和wCDM模型的贝叶斯因子，分别使用均匀先验和基于Planck观测的正态先验。

Result: 在均匀先验下，贝叶斯因子接近1，说明R_h=ct与ΛCDM/wCDM等效；在Planck正态先验下，R_h=ct显著优于ΛCDM，略优于wCDM。

Conclusion: R_h=ct模型在符合当前高精度宇宙学先验（如Planck）时具有较强竞争力，挑战标准宇宙学模型的唯一性。

Abstract: We complement a recent analysis comparing $R_\mathrm{h}=ct$ with $Λ$CDM/$w$CDM using HII galaxies and giant extragalactic HII regions, by carrying out Bayesian model comparison. For this purpose, we calculate the Bayes factors for $R_\mathrm{h}=ct$ compared to flat $Λ$CDM/$w$CDM using the same dataset. When we use uniform priors on cosmological parameters, we find that the Bayes factors are close to 1, implying that $R_\mathrm{h}=ct$ is equally favored compared to $Λ$CDM/$w$CDM. However, when we use normal priors on cosmological parameters based on Planck cosmology, we find that $R_\mathrm{h}=ct$ is strongly favored over flat $Λ$CDM, while $R_\mathrm{h}=ct$ is marginally favored over flat $w$CDM.

</details>


### [135] [Investigating the $H_0$ Tension and Expansion-History Mismatch with Diverse Dark Energy Parametrization Frameworks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28391)
*Upala Mukhopadhyay,Purba Mukherjee,Alexandre Tkatchenko*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了ΛCDM模型中H₀张力的红移起源，通过三种暗能量参数化模型分析发现，仅压力密度参数化能将H₀张力降至~2.7σ，且偏差主要集中在低红移（z≈0.51, 0.706），表明晚期修改仅重塑而非彻底解决张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ΛCDM模型虽成功但存在H₀张力等长期未解问题，亟需定位张力在宇宙膨胀历史中的具体起源红移区间。

Method: 采用三种基于暗能量状态方程、压力密度和尺度因子的唯象参数化模型，结合Planck（早期）、Pantheon+（含/不含SH0ES校准）和DESI（晚期）数据，约束参数并重构H(z)演化。

Result: ΛCDM在全红移范围均有偏差；其余模型将主要偏差移向低红移；压力密度参数化使H₀张力降至~2.7σ；DESI DR2在z=0.51和0.706处显示显著H(z)偏离，高红移则一致；不同参数化下暗能量动力学行为明显不同。

Conclusion: H₀张力根源更可能与低红移物理相关，但当前晚期修改仅能重塑H(z)失配的红移依赖性，无法根本解决张力；早期与晚期探针对暗能量本质的描述仍存在本质不一致。

Abstract: The $Λ$CDM model successfully explains a wide range of cosmological observations; however, persistent discrepancies most notably the $H_0$ tension between early and late time measurements challenge its completeness. No proposed extension has yet resolved this tension while retaining the overall success of $Λ$CDM. In this work, we investigate whether the $H_0$ tension can be associated with a specific epoch in the cosmic expansion history and identify the redshift range most relevant for understanding its origin. In addition to the cosmological constant, we consider three phenomenological models based on general parametrizations of key quantities governing cosmic expansion: the dark energy (DE) equation of state, the DE pressure density, and the scale factor. Using early time Planck data and late time Pantheon+ (with and without SH0ES calibration) and DESI measurements, we constrain model parameters and examine the evolution of the Hubble parameter $H(z)$. We find that $Λ$CDM exhibits discrepancies across all redshifts, whereas the other models shift the dominant deviations toward low redshifts. Among the models considered, the pressure density parametrization alleviates the $H_0$ tension, reducing it to $\sim 2.7σ$, while the other models do not provide significant improvement. A detailed analysis of DESI DR2 data further reveals notable deviations in $H(z)$ at $z=0.51$ and 0.706, whereas higher redshift measurements remain consistent within $1σ$. These results suggest that late-time modifications primarily reshape the redshift dependence of the mismatch in $H(z)$ rather than fully resolve it, in the absence of systematic effects. Furthermore, the reconstructed DE dynamics exhibit qualitatively distinct behaviors across parametrizations, highlighting a persistent inconsistency between early and late Universe probes in describing the nature of DE.

</details>


### [136] [Estimation and mitigation of foregrounds in projected kSZ velocity reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28746)
*Carmen Embil Villagra,Fiona McCarthy,Antón Baleato Lizancos,Blake D. Sherwin,Anthony Challinor*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了kSZ效应在宇宙学中的应用，特别是其在重建大尺度速度场和探测原初非高斯性方面的潜力，并提出了一种能消除前景污染的奇偶性估计器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着kSZ速度重建测量灵敏度的提高，CMB图中星系外前景污染等系统效应变得越来越重要，需要研究其对kSZ重建速度-星系交叉相关性的偏差影响。

Method: 使用晕模型描述热SZ效应和宇宙红外背景的前景贡献，并引入一种基于层析速度-星系相关性的反对称组合构建的奇偶性估计器，在Limber近似下理论上完全消除前景污染。

Result: 该奇偶性估计器在ACT DR6温度图与DESI Legacy Imaging Survey星系数据上的应用显示，信号检测显著提升至11σ，幅度与近期研究一致。

Conclusion: 所提出的奇偶性估计器可有效消除前景污染，同时完整保留宇宙学信号且不损失信噪比，显著提升了kSZ速度-星系相关性测量的精度与可靠性。

Abstract: The kSZ effect has recently emerged as a powerful probe for precision cosmology through its ability to reconstruct the large-scale velocity field. In particular, the kSZ-reconstructed velocity-galaxy cross-correlation is sensitive to signatures of primordial non-Gaussianity through its imprint on the galaxy bias. The kSZ velocity reconstruction is performed using small-scale information from CMB temperature and galaxy overdensities. As the sensitivity of these measurements improves, systematic effects such as extragalactic foreground contamination present in CMB maps become increasingly important. We present a study of foreground biases to the kSZ-reconstructed velocity-galaxy cross-correlation. We derive the relevant foreground contributions from the thermal Sunyaev-Zel'dovich effect and the cosmic infrared background, modeling them using a halo model description of the dominant one- and two-halo terms. We compare our analytic predictions to measurements obtained using ACT DR6 temperature maps and DESI Legacy Imaging Survey galaxies, finding qualitative agreement. We introduce a parity-odd estimator constructed from antisymmetric combinations of tomographic velocity-galaxy correlations and show analytically that, under the Limber approximation, this estimator entirely cancels the foreground contamination while preserving the full cosmological signal without loss of signal-to-noise. Finally, we apply this parity-odd estimator to the data combination mentioned above and show that the fit to the velocity-galaxy correlation is dramatically improved compared to the analysis without mitigation; our estimator detects the signal at 11$σ$, with an amplitude consistent with recent studies.

</details>


### [137] [Cosmic Shear in Effective Field Theory at Two-Loop Order: Revisiting $S_8$ in Dark Energy Survey Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28761)
*Shi-Fan Chen,Joseph DeRose,Mikhail M. Ivanov,Oliver H. E. Philcox*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用两环有效场论（EFT）方法对DES-Y3宇宙剪切数据进行首次一致分析，通过透镜计数项展开和自旋-2 EFT描述星系内禀对齐，有效缓解了重子物理带来的系统误差，得到具有竞争力的S8约束，并表明宇宙剪切在当前尺度下高度可扰动，为未来巡天实验探测新物理提供了新机遇。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙剪切是限制宇宙学参数的重要探针，但其精度受限于对重子天体物理效应的理解，导致大量小尺度信息无法使用。

Method: 采用两环阶有效场论（EFT）建模宇宙剪切功率谱，引入透镜计数项（lensing-counterterm）处理小尺度非线性敏感性，并用自旋-2 EFT描述星系内禀对齐（IA）；结合DES-Y3剪切数据、BAO、CMB及超新星数据进行联合拟合。

Result: 得到S8 = 0.783^{+0.038}_{-0.031}（仅DES-Y3），加入BAO后为0.802^{+0.031}_{-0.026}；联合多探针后在动力学暗能量模型中得S8 = 0.824 ± 0.029，未见S8张力。

Conclusion: 宇宙剪切在可用尺度上基本处于微扰区，两环EFT可高精度建模，显著降低重子系统误差；该框架支持在Roman、Euclid、LSST等未来巡天中开展新物理检验与精确宇宙学测量。

Abstract: Cosmic shear is a powerful probe of cosmological distances, matter abundance and clustering in the low-redshift Universe. Cosmological parameter extraction from cosmic shear data is limited by our understanding of baryonic astrophysics, which severely restricts the range of scales used in such analyses. We show that the remaining scales are largely perturbative and can be accurately described with two-loop effective field theory (EFT) predictions. We present the first consistent analysis of the public cosmic shear data from the DES-Y3 catalogs in EFT at the two-loop order, renormalizing small-scale sensitivity in cosmic-shear predictions via a lensing-counterterm expansion and accounting for the intrinsic alignments of galaxies with spin-2 EFT predictions. We constrain the lensing amplitude competitively with standard (empirically-modeled) methods, finding $S_8 = 0.783^{+0.038}_{-0.031}$ ($S_8 = 0.802^{+0.031}_{-0.026}$ with BAO). The perturbativity of cosmic shear suggests novel opportunities for testing new physics with ongoing and upcoming cosmic shear experiments like Roman, Euclid, and LSST. As an example, we derive matter clustering constraints within the dynamical dark energy model from a combination of our DES-EFT cosmic shear likelihood, early-universe CMB priors, DESI BAO, and supernovae data, finding $S_8 = 0.824\pm 0.029$, indicating no $S_8$ tension in the growth of cosmic structure regardless of the underlying cosmological model and expansion history.

</details>
